### ExtendType

Ƭ **ExtendType**<`TProps`\>: [`ExtendValue`](akashaproject_design_system._internal_.md#extendvalue)<`TProps`\> \| [`ExtendFn`](akashaproject_design_system._internal_.md#extendfn)<`TProps`\>

ExtendType represents the type for `extend` values in the theme.

Acceptable values for `extend` are one of:

* A string containing css
* An array of styled-components interpolations (usually returned by the styled-components `css` helper function)
* A function taking props and returning one of the above values

#### Type parameters

| Name | Type |
| :------ | :------ |
| `TProps` | [`Record`](akashaproject_design_system._internal_.md#record)<`string`, `any`\> |

#### Defined in

ui/design/node_modules/grommet/themes/base.d.ts:71

### ExtendValue

Ƭ **ExtendValue**<`TProps`\>: `string` \| [`FlattenSimpleInterpolation`](akashaproject_design_system._internal_.md#flattensimpleinterpolation) \| [`FlattenInterpolation`](akashaproject_design_system._internal_.md#flatteninterpolation)<[`ExtendProps`](akashaproject_design_system._internal_.md#extendprops)<`TProps`\>\>

ExtendValue represents a valid `extend` value, which can be a CSS string or a
styled-components interpolation. In the theme an ExtendValue can be provided
directly to `extend` or it can be computed as the result of an ExtendFn.
